## **Mirad Thesaurus**

Welcome to **Mirad Thesaurus** , a thematically-ordered vocabulary of Mirad, a serious constructed language. This book is an accompaniment to Mirad Grammar.

Table of Contents

- Universe • Nature • Weather • Flora • Fauna • Human Body • Clothing • Society • Family • Health • Home • Food • City Life • Commerce • School • Mathematics

- Government • Technology • Geography • Military • Arts and Entertainment • Religion • Mirad Grammar

## **Atmosphere**

- **maalyen jaden** = _weather prediction_

- **maalyen jwaden** = _weather warning_

Words with the **f...b** pattern refer to plants, fruits, and nuts; those with the **v...b** pattern refer to grasses and cereals; and those with **v...l** refer to vegetables.

## **Colors**

Most color names in Mirad are derived from flowers, fruits, or other things in nature. The basic word skeleton is **v...za** .

|**COLOR**|**MIRAD**<br>**COLORNAME**|**ENGLISH**<br>**COLORNAME**|**DERIVATION**|
|---|---|---|---|
||**avoza**|_white_|**avos**=_lily_|
||**evoza**|_yellow_|**evos**=_narcissus_|
||**ivoza**|_red_|**ivos**=_poppy_|
||**uvoza**|_pink_|**uvos**=_rose_|
||**yovoza**|_blue_|**yovos**=_cornfower_|
||**yavoza**|_mauve_|**yavos**=_mallow fower_|
||**yevoza**|_lilac_|**yevos**=_lilac_|
||**yivoza**|_purple_|**yivos**=_violet_|
||**yoivoza**|_indigo_|**yovos**+**yivos**=_blue violet_|
||**yuvoza**|_marigold_|**yuvos**=_marigold_|
||**lyuvoza**|_vivid purple_|**lyuvos**=_orchid_|
||**vaza**|_green_|**vab**=_grass_|
||**moza**|_black_|**mon**=_dark_|
||**eymoza**|_gray_|**eymon**=_shade_|
||**meza**|_brown_|**mel**=_dirt_|
||**dyofeza**|_chocolate_|**dyofel**=_cocoa_|
||**lafeza**|_orange_|**lafeb**=_orange_|

Page 44

||**utayeza**|_beige_|**utayef**=_wool_|
|---|---|---|---|
||**kafeza**|_olive_|**kafeb**=_olive_|
||**lipiza**|_salmon_|**lipit**=_salmon_|

Dark versions of a color have the format **vy...za** , while lighter or _-ish_ forms have the format **v...yza** , e.g.:

- **vaza** = _green_

- **vayza** = _light green, greenish_

- **vyaza** = _dark green_

## **Fauna**

## **Fauna**

The names of animals in Mirad all contain the letters **p** , meaning _mobile_ , and end in the letter **t** for _creature_ . The ordinal vowel in the stem relates to a geophysical domain, such as air, water, land, or combinations of these.

• **pot** = _animal_ • **pet** = _land animal_ • **pit** = _fish_ • **pyot** = _wild_ • **pyet** = _reptile_ • **pyit** = _predatory or animal_ • **payet** = _flying game fish reptile_ • **piit** = _crustacean_ • **pelt** = _insect_ • **piyet** = _batrachian_ • **pat** = _bird_ • **peyet** = _worm_ • **peit** = _marine_ • **pyat** = _bird of_ • **plet** = _marsupial mammal prey, raptor_ • **pyeit** = _mollusk_ • **piat** = _aquatic bird_ • **pelat** = _flying insect_

Note the following details from the above chart:

- Stems of all flying creatures (except reptiles) end in **-at**

-

- Stems of birds of prey or raptors end in **-yat** .

- Stems of aquatic birds end in **-iat** .

- Stem of flying insects end in **-lat** .

-

- Stems of all land animals and non-flying insects end in **-ot** or **-et** .

-

- Wild land animals end in **-yot** .

- Less wild land animals end in **-ot** .

- Less wild aquatic land animals end in **-iot** .

- Domesticated land animals end in **-et** .

-

- Non-flying reptiles end in **-yet** .

-

- Flying reptiles end in **-ayet** .

-

- Amphibians or batrachians end in **-iyet** .

- Marsuplials end in **-let** .

- Non-flying insects end in **-elt** .

-

- Worms end in **-eyet** .

-

- All sea and river creatures end in **-it** , especially fish proper.

-

- Game or predatory fish end in **-yit** .

- Crustaceans or shellfish end in **-iit** .

-

- Marine mammals end in **-eit** . • Mollusks end in **-yeit** .

- The feminine counterpart of animals is derived by following the last stem vowel with **-y-** . • The offspring of an animal is derived by suffixing **-ud** to the stem.

- A small version of an animal is derved by suffixing **-og** to the stem.

-

- A pet version of an animal is derived by suffixing **-if** to the stem.

Page 46

Page 56

## **Human Body**

## **Human Body**

- **tob** = _human_

- **tab** = _body_

- • **teb** = _head_ • **tib** = _trunk_ • **tub** = _arm_ • **tyob** = _leg_

- **top** = _soul_

- • **tap** = _physique_ • **tep** = _mind_

- **tip** = _sentiment_

The stem of body part words begin with **t** , signifying a _human_ or _live creature_ , and end with **b** , meaning _organism_ . Words referring to non-tangible parts begin with **t** and end in **p** .

The words are derived from the base word **tob** and descend organizationally.

## **Clothing**

## **Clothing**

- **tof** = _clothes_

- **taf** = _suit_

- • **tef** = _hat_ • **tif** = _coat_ • **tuf** = _sleeve_ • **tyof** = _pants_ • **tyoyaf** = _shoe_

- **nof** = _cloth_

- • **naf** = _fabric_

- **nef** = _knit_

- **nif** = _yarn_

- **nuf** = _button_

- **nyof** = _film_

- **nyaf** = _knot_

- **nyef** = _mesh, bag_

- • **nyif** = _cord_ • **nyuf** = _package_

The stem of clothing items echos the body part they cover (see Human Body. Basically, the final **b** ( _organism_ ) of the body part is changed to an **f** ( _textile_ ) or **v** for softer linen equivalents. The item worn by women is formed by infixing a **y** before the **f** or **v** stem-final consonant. The stem of the commercial materials from which clothes are made begins in **n** .

- **aber** = _to put on_

- **finagser** = _to fit_ ( **Hia tef voy finagse.** = _This hat does not fit._ )

   - **abyoxer ota tofi** = _to hang up one's clothes_

## **Textiles**

Words having to do with commercial textiles begin with **n** , meaning _commercial_ and end in **f** or **v** .

- **nif** = _yarn, fiber_

- • **niyf** = _filament_ • **niv** = _thread_ • **niiv** = _strand_

## **Family**

## **Core Words**

Notice that kinship terms are gender-neutral unless there is a **w** before the root syllable vowel (indicating male-specific) or a **y** following the root syllable vowel (indicating female-specific).

## T...D Words

|**tod....****_family_**|**MALE**|**FEMALE**|
|---|---|---|
|**tad**...._spouse_|**twad**...._husband_|**tayd**...._wife_|
|**ted**...._parent_|**twed**...._father_|**teyd**...._mother_|
|**tid**...._sibling_|**twid**...._brother_|**tiyd**...._sister_|
|**tud**...._child_|**twud**...._son_|**tuyd**...._daughter_|

## **Genealogical Prefixes**

Prefixes or word elements used to modify the above core words:

Genealogical Prefixes

**to-** .... _god-_ (as in _godson_ )

**ta-** .... _-in-law, through marriage_ **te-** .... _father's_ **ti-** .... _sibling's_ **tu-** .... _child's_ **taj-** .... _birth-, real_ **otaj-, ifbi-** .... _foster, adopted_ **ij-** .... _first, original_ **aj-** .... _ex-, former_ **ej-** .... _current, step-, half-_ **oj-** .... _future, -to-be_ **aa** .... _first_ **ea** .... _second_ **yiba** .... _distant_ **aa yiba** .... _first-removed_ **ea yiba** .... _second-removed_ **ota-** .... _out-of-wedlock, bastard_ **oyted-** .... _orphan(ed), without parents_ **oytad-** .... _unmarried, without spouse_ **oytud-** .... _childless, without child, barren_ **tiibil-** .... _blood-_

## **Kinship Terms**

Kinship Terms Formed from the Above Core Words and Prefixed Elements

Page 99

Kinship Terms

|**GENDER-NEUTRAL**|**MALE**|**FEMALE**|
|---|---|---|

|**tyez**...._magic_|**tyezun**...._magic act_|**tyezut**...._magician_|**tyezem**...._magic venue_|

As for venues, if it's a building, it ends in **-am** (like _theater_ ); if a hall or gallery, **-em** ; if a studio, **-im** ; if a booth, **-um** .

The female version of persons is derived by preceding the final **-t** with a **y** ( **dizuyt** .... _comedienne_ ).

## **Religion**

The most important roots in this sphere are:

- **fya-** .... _holy, sacred_

- **fye-** .... _mythical, mystical, fanciful_

- **fyo-** .... _evil, profane, unholy_

Here is a table showing the most important words using these roots:

Religous/ Mythical / Diabolical Terms

|**HOLY**|**MYSTICAL**|**UNHOLY**|
|---|---|---|
|**fyaa**...._holy, sacred_|**fyea**...._mythical, mystical, fanciful_|**fyoa**...._evil, profane, unholy_|
|**fyat**...._saint_|**fyet**...._ghost, wight, sprite_|**fyot**...._demon_|
|**fyamir**...._heaven_|**fyemir**...._fantasy world_|**fyomir**...._underworld, hell_|
|**fyadin**...._gospel_|**fyedin**...._fairytale_||
|**fyad**...._blessing_|**fyed**...._spell_|**fyod**...._curse_|
|**fyadeuz**...._hymn_|**fyedeuz**...._skirl, incantation_||
|**fyasun**...._idol_|**fyesun**...._talisman_|**fyosun**...._taboo_|
|**fyax**...._holy deed_||**fyox**...._sin_|
|**fyatop**...._angel_|**fyetop**...._ghost, phantom_|**fyotop**...._devil, evil spirit_|
